 sheersh adaalat registry ke anusaar pariyojna dhire-dhire lagu kii jaaegi or pehali baar main pratham paanch adaalaton main sirf soochibaddh naye maamalon ko nyaayadhish ek disple par dekh sakenge
 The Registry said that all the High Courts in the country have been given a login ID to upload digital records in the prescribed format
 sheersh adaalat registry ne kaha ki supreme court ne adaalat ko paperles banane ke liye sari taiyaari kar rakhi hai
 Since the concept of paperless courts involves many technical and working issues, it has to be gradually implemented
 darasal adhivaktaaon or nyaayadhishon ke kaamkaaj kaa yah nayaa tarika hoga
 It was also told that after launching the Integrated Case Management Information System (ICMIS) of the Supreme Court, various high courts in the country have uploaded a large number of case files on it
 ucchtam nyaayalay registry sabhi ucch nyaayalayon se baatcheet kar rahaa he
 Even video conferences were held with the nodal officers of the High Courts
 jiskaa aakhri lakshya adaalat ko paperles bananaa he
 Now the Supreme Court will also go paperless and go digital
 supreme court electronic madhyam se hoicourt or trial court ke record hasil kar legaa
 So that lawyers and parties will get rid of thick documents
